r3641 | olly98 | 2011-08-24 03:02:28 -0600 (Wed, 24 Aug 2011) | 8 lines

Added highlighting in preview area for search text (based on patch 3121914 by Maximilian Lengsfeld).

The "transport" of the words to search has been modified to conform to the infrastructure established by patch 3117881.
SearchExpressionKeyParser is NOT used, but the SearchTextListener interface directly passing the keywords.
The issue with this approach is that the search format "field=keyword" does not work. "field=keyword" is tried to be highlighted
and not "keyword" everywhere (as suggested by the patch).

Only the preview panel is highlighted, other layouts (export, find duplicates, ...) are not affected.

r2441 | lpatton | 2007-10-24 10:06:05 -0600 (Wed, 24 Oct 2007) | 8 lines

Re-worked SQL export user interface.  Now, there are two buttons -- one for
collecting the DB strings from the user, and another for performing the
export.  When an export is requested, the user will be prompted for the
DB strings if jabref doesn't already have them.   If jabref has valid DB
strings, the user will not be prompted for anything.  The use can change
the DB strings by clicking the "Connect to External DB" button or File
menu option.

r2117 | udvranto | 2007-06-19 15:32:56 -0600 (Tue, 19 Jun 2007) | 2 lines

Charformat is made optional using the CHARFORMAT boolean variable. Charformat causes unicode characters to become html encoded. This is safe if there is some invalid xml character in the file. But it looks ugly. So the xml unsafe characters are removed using another function. Thus we don't need char format anymore.

r1333 | sebwills | 2005-12-08 09:08:55 -0600 (Thu, 08 Dec 2005) | 8 lines

Fix incorrect order of setVisible and toFront, which was causing the splash
screen to appear minimized or behind other windows on some X servers (e.g.
VNC, NX). In some cases this was causing deadlock since splash() waited for
a paint event that would never come.

As an additional safety measure, add a timeout of 5 seconds in case the
paint event never comes.
